<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_338b29a6-b6ec-452b-8cb3-f6ef56cf64af'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</script>

  <span id="freeText6285924479605556593" style="display:none"><b> Riddle me this...</b><br /><i>“I am neither dead, nor alive, and I’m not something little Madison can hide.<br />But you will be dead, by the time this is done...<br />the timer starts now, and the games have just begun…”</i><br /><br />Madison Montgomery comes from money and power, but when someone close to her commits the ultimate crime, Madison must live with her tainted name for the rest of her life. When she begins Riverside Preparatory Academy, the private school her father has swept her into in The Hamptons, she hopes for a fresh start. What she wasn't hoping for was the pack of bad boys who run the school; ten, to be exact. When Madison gains the attention of their leader, Bishop Vincent Hayes, a whole new world that she didn't think existed is exposed to her. A whole world that starts and ends with The Elite Kings Club and these boys, are about to flip her world upside down. Secrets are overflowing and family lies are about to be exposed. Is there more to Madison Montgomery than even she knows?</span>

          </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1821741962" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6715601615523813358">Just going to post this review and then run and hide. =D<br/><br/><a href='http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/h_zpstbtxijxb.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488931785ra/22169651.gif' alt='hide photo h_zpstbtxijxb.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I won't go into extreme detail about what didn't work for me. I decided to read this because the blurb sounded interesting with promises of 'insane characters and an insane story', even though I don't really read 'dark' reads anymore. And this is mainly because it’s been rare for me to come across a dark story where the characters seem believable and the situations aren’t just absurd and/or convenient. And that is a big part of the reas</span>
  <span id="freeText6715601615523813358" style="display:none">Just going to post this review and then run and hide. =D<br><br><a href="http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/h_zpstbtxijxb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488931785ra/22169651.gif" alt="hide photo h_zpstbtxijxb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I won't go into extreme detail about what didn't work for me. I decided to read this because the blurb sounded interesting with promises of 'insane characters and an insane story', even though I don't really read 'dark' reads anymore. And this is mainly because it’s been rare for me to come across a dark story where the characters seem believable and the situations aren’t just absurd and/or convenient. And that is a big part of the reason why I didn’t enjoy this book.<br><br>I did like the mystery and intrigue. The premise had potential, but for ME, the execution was <u>way off.</u><br><br>The writing itself could have done with a REALLY GOOD amount of editing. It was repetitive, had a lot of grammatical errors, and the pacing just felt off. The storyline was all over the place. In some places there was just a huge info dump with a lot of unnecessary details and filler. And then there were times where I could have used more background information or more detail. There were also things the characters thought or said that made absolutely no sense and contradicted something that was previously stated.<br><br>The characters were way too absurd and immature. I realize these are high school students, but that doesn't mean they need to be written in such an over the top manner. Especially when you're trying to appeal to an adult crowd. I also couldn't connect with any of them. I found the heroine to be daft and lacked common sense and the heroes felt like a stereotyped clichéd version of what high school bad boys should be.<br><br>Clearly this wasn’t for me, but I maybe others will enjoy this more than I did. <br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Find Me On:<br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thecrazyworldofabooklover/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/profile.php?id=100009277089211" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Page</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover/" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://twitter.com/_StephDeMarco_" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a></span>

<div id="review_1934262473" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1934262473" />
    <a title="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog"><img alt="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471840369p2/37057510.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1934262473?book_show_action=true">Mar 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" href="/user/show/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog">Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1934262473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12929092506212023690">4.5 stars <br/><br/>I'm about to binge the rest of this series, so I decided to reread this before I wound up confused as fuck. Lol I'm so ready now for whatever awaits!! Let the mindfucking begin! 🙌🏻😂<br/><br/><a href='http://s1303.photobucket.com/user/majikmommie/media/PicsArt_03-07-08.39.30_zpsjfhpv1sv.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488941853i/22170455._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo PicsArt_03-07-08.39.30_zpsjfhpv1sv.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>"To stories that fuck you so hard you’ll need a cigarette.<br/>This is one of those stories."- Amo Jones</i><br/><br/>I’m sitting here trying to figure out how to write this review. What can I tell you that will be just enough to peak your interest, but not enough to ruin the twists or the suspense, give you the wrong idea</span>
  <span id="freeText12929092506212023690" style="display:none">4.5 stars <br><br>I'm about to binge the rest of this series, so I decided to reread this before I wound up confused as fuck. Lol I'm so ready now for whatever awaits!! Let the mindfucking begin! 🙌🏻😂<br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/user/majikmommie/media/PicsArt_03-07-08.39.30_zpsjfhpv1sv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488941853i/22170455._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_03-07-08.39.30_zpsjfhpv1sv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>"To stories that fuck you so hard you’ll need a cigarette.<br>This is one of those stories."- Amo Jones</i><br><br>I’m sitting here trying to figure out how to write this review. What can I tell you that will be just enough to peak your interest, but not enough to ruin the twists or the suspense, give you the wrong idea, or make me sound insane? I’m thinking the answer is probably not much. Yet, that’s what I have to do, so here goes nothing!<br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/user/majikmommie/media/pagebreak_zpscaredzya.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487300146i/21997578._SX540_.png" alt=" photo pagebreak_zpscaredzya.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Madison Montgomery’s father moved them to a new town, because he found “the one”...again. Madi hoped that moving to a new city would let her leave behind the whispers and rumors surrounding her family. When your mother finds out your father is cheating on her and murders the homewrecker with YOUR gun before killing herself, people tend to talk. It’s the kind of thing that at the least intrigues others. Unfortunately, for Madi, it’s also the kind of thing that follows you wherever you go. <br><br>Trying to blend in like she wants to turns out to be pretty impossible. She does manage to make one good friend, Tatum, at school which is more than she can usually say for herself. Tatum warns her to be careful when she captures the attention of a group of 10 hot as hell guys that are shrouded in mystery. Everyone wants them, wants to be them, and/or is terrified of them. According to the rumor mill, they supposedly belong to a secret club of some sort called, The Elite Kings Club. No one knows for sure what it is just that it has something to do with their lineage. The disappearance of Bishop’s ex girlfriend, Khales, is another topic of discussion among their student body.<br><br> <a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/user/majikmommie/media/PicsArt_03-07-08.40.34_zpsqehnersv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488941853i/22170456._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_03-07-08.40.34_zpsqehnersv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Madi soon discovers that staying away from the boys simply isn’t going to happen. Not only does she draw the eye of their gorgeous leader, Bishop, but one of the guys, Nate, is actually her new stepbrother. Some of the group automatically acts like they can’t stand her, but they also stand guard over her at almost all times.<br><br> At first, Madi thinks the rumors are just that; however, the more time she spends with the boys, the more she starts to think there is some truth to all the rumors. Everything is a secret, they keep referring to being part of a game, and do all sorts of other strange things that would make anyone question what the hell was going on. There are so many questions she wants answers to. There are so many questions YOU will want answers to. What ever happened to Khales? Why did Bishop’s father mistake her for someone else? Why does Brantley show such animosity towards her even though they just met? Why do they think she knows something that she doesn’t? What part of their life is this game they keep talking about, and what is real? Honestly, that isn’t anywhere near the amount of questions you will have while reading this or even after it’s over, but that’s all I can say without spoiling anything.<br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/user/majikmommie/media/PicsArt_03-07-08.41.45_zps9wduwepq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488941853i/22170457._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_03-07-08.41.45_zps9wduwepq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/user/majikmommie/media/pagebreak_zpscaredzya.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487300146i/21997578._SX540_.png" alt=" photo pagebreak_zpscaredzya.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What did I think of The Silver Swan? Overall, it is a unique, intriguing, and captivating read. I was constantly questioning everything and waiting for the other shoe to drop. The whole time I read, the phrase “What the fuck?” was on loop in my head. I love books that keep me guessing, and this one definitely did that. I also love asshole alphas, and Bishop is a delicious one.<br><br>Did I have any issues with it? Sure. I think Madi was a little too easy when it came to Bishop and letting the boys slide for their erratic/totally messed up behavior. Either way, it made the book more entertaining for me, so I wasn’t bothered by it. LOL Again, that’s all I can really say without revealing too much.<br><br>Would I recommend it? Yes! If you like messed up stories full of mystery, asshole alphas, and suspense, with some hot sex thrown in for good measure, this one is for you. I will warn you that while you will get answers to some of your questions, you will be left with even more, so if you don’t like cliffhangers, you may want to wait until the next book comes out to read this one. However, the cliffhanger didn’t bother me all that much to be honest. I am so glad that I decided to read this book, and I can’t wait to see what is going to happen next!<br><br><a href="http://chatterbooksbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <b>
    <i>Madison Mon</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText17808077189324415342" style="display:none"><b>4.75 "Who the fuck are you all?" stars</b><br><br>WHOA!!!! Fuckin wow!!!<br><br>Let's just say this book could be described as a well blended mixture of <b>Penelope Douglas's</b> <i>Corrupt</i>, <b>Erin Watt</b>'s <i>The Royals</i> series and <b>Tijan</b>'s <i>Fallen Crest High</i> brought onto a higher level of potency...<br><br>and I won't even try to go into re-telling the story, cause it would not do it justice, so I'm gonna borrow Amo's blurb, cause it simply says it ALL and yet reveals NOT ONE SINGLE THING you should NOT know beforehand...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Madison Montgomery comes from money and power, but when someone close to her commits the ultimate crime, Madison must live with her tainted name for the rest of her life. When she begins Riverside Preparatory Academy, the private school her father has swept her into in The Hamptons, she hopes for a fresh start. What she wasn't hoping for was the pack of bad boys who run the school; ten, to be exact. When Madison gains the attention of their leader, Bishop Vincent Hayes, a whole new world that she didn't think existed is exposed to her. A whole world that starts and ends with The Elite Kings Club and these boys, are about to flip her world upside down. Secrets are overflowing and family lies are about to be exposed. Is there more to Madison Montgomery than even she knows?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488478366i/22121113._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Damn, I just loved the <b>angsty, anticipating feeling and a constant suspense I got from the story..</b><br>it's the very feeling that kept me <b>on the edge, alive, itchy and vivid</b>...questioning everything and everyone, and yet I had to keep firmly in mind that they are 17 years old...gah<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488477921i/22121055._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The <b>characters were intriguing</b> and very unlike the teens around you, duh?! I loved how they were <b>multi-layered and complex, strong and vulnerable at the same time, wild/reckless yet serious...</b><br><br><b>Madison</b> - damn, I loved her. Badass, smart, mouthy, out-spoken, bold yet vulnerable and eager for love...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488478092i/22121082._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and <b>Bishop</b>, you little motherfucker, him and the rest of his little gang...untamed, spoiled, above everyone and everything...and yet behind the screen, they too play the parts they DO NOT want to play, per se BUT instead they were merely brought into it...by blood...tradition, money, greed, scrupules...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488452540ra/22116397.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and all the <b>lies and secrets bring the sour taste of betrayal and self-doubt</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488478240i/22121102._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Inspite of these little issues i had along the way with certain pin points in the story, without a doubt, <b> there's a <i>constant rush, the thrill, the suspense, the mystery eating away the last sensible thought leaving me in a confused and utterly vivid mess with soooo many questions...</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488292129ra/22098627.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>and I need the next book, like NOW!</b><br><br><br>***ARC kindely given by the author <b>Amo Jones</b> in exchange for and honest review***</b></span>

  <span id="freeText12244120493549971918" style="display:none">Many people loved this book, So I'm going to skip the praise (you can read plenty of it elsewhere). i had high hopes for this one, The blurb was so damn good. Unfortunately, the whole story didn't work for me. The characters were mean, Super creepy and absurd. And Of course, The author didn't offer any explanation whatsoever, Nada, Nothing. *SIGH*<br /><br />Overall, I think this story had potential, and this could have been a much better book.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4361629076415964884"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>

For more info on this challenge, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/16216645-urr-s-new-years-2018-romance-reading-challenge' rel='nofollow noopener'>click here</a>. 💙<br/><br/><br/><br/>We all have some friends whose opinions about books are so similar to ours that if they rate a book highly, we immediately zoom out to the Kindle Store to buy it. I know I do. But there are also some bloggers out there whose tastes are so antithetical to </span>
  <span id="freeText4361629076415964884" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>💙 I read this for the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/187063-unapologetic-romance-readers" rel="nofollow noopener">Unapologetic Romance Readers</a>' <b>New Years 2018 Reading Challenge</b>, for the category of: <i>Millionaire/Billionaire Romance</i>. For more info on this challenge, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/16216645-urr-s-new-years-2018-romance-reading-challenge" rel="nofollow noopener">click here</a>. 💙<br><br><br><br>We all have some friends whose opinions about books are so similar to ours that if they rate a book highly, we immediately zoom out to the Kindle Store to buy it. I know I do. But there are also some bloggers out there whose tastes are so antithetical to mine that if I see that they have given a book five stars, it automatically goes on my internal do-not-buy list.<br><br><br><br>This happened in the case of THE SILVER SWAN, but unfortunately, I had already downloaded it from the Kindle Store, and I figured that maybe it could be good. Sometimes I like dark smutty stories, if they're dark and smutty enough. But they have to be well-written and they have to be interesting.<br><br><br><br>THE SILVER SWAN was neither.<br><br><br><br>THE SILVER SWAN kind of feels like it was heavily influenced by Penelope Douglas's <i>Devil's Night </i>series and Erin Watt's PAPER PRINCESS. The main character, Madi, is a "troubled" rich girl whose mother killed her husband's mistress before killing herself with one of Madi's own guns (Madi's a gun nut). As a fresh start, her father has enrolled her in a rich kid's school in a rich kid area, in the hope that such richy richness will magically cure her psychological problems, because I guess therapy is just another word for Aston Martin. *eye roll* Dad of the Year is an award that this man will not be getting, because he is so taken with his new wife that he neglected to inform his daughter that her step-mom has a step-brother her age, whose room is next to hers - and oh, yeah, he's a pervert.<br><br><br><br>Once at her new school, things take a turn for the TWILIGHT where Madi ends up with a Jessica of her own, only this Jessica is named Tatum and is rich as sin. She also meets ten Edwards, only these Edwards are more like his Christian Grey incarnation, if Christian Grey was a sleazy seventeen-year-old who divides his free time between lurking outside expensive nightclubs and beating off. All of them are immediately intrigued by her, even though their attention cannot be captured by any SINGLE girl, such is the immense power of their collective testosterone. Plot bonus: pervy step-brother is a member of this dicktastic elite collective, redundantly known as the Elite Kings.<br><br><br><br>The Kings waste no time in stalking Madi, sexually harassing Madi, threatening Madi with rape, with bodily harm, and even with murder. They keep making all of these vague threats about how she will die soon, or that there is a secret about her that they cannot share (thanks for the helpful info, guys). The most unstable Christian Grey of them all, Bishop, even tells her that he thinks she has a sexy spine and wants to break it, and this is of course after he threatens to disembowel her right before they have sex - yet again. I suppose if you find the relationship between Harley Quinn and the Joker healthy, you would see no problem with this, and it seems like Madi does, so yay for her, I guess?<br><br><br><br>As a reader of bodice rippers, I am not a stranger to OTT smut and wtfery, and when it is done well I will even tolerate it in modern erotica. Case in point: PAPER PRINCESS and, most recently, A. Zavarelli's CROW, a book that I thought I would hate and ended up loving instead. I had hoped that something similar might happen with THE SILVER SWAN, but I ended up being pretty fed up with the book because of what I perceived to be lazy writing (highly repetitive descriptions, for example: "eyes filled with mischief" occurring in two succeeding paragraphs; lots of typos) and way too many asides. The obsession with food in this book is particularly curious, with Madi constantly telling us what she wants to eat or is currently eating, and exactly how much progress she is making as she continues to eat or obtain this food in question, whether it's a sandwich, an apple, Krispey Kremes, or enough Burger King to "feed half a state."<br><br><br><br>I also didn't particularly care for Madi, and her "I'm not like other girls" attitude was particularly jarring and irritating, as was her vapid, superficial lifestyle and her easy judgment of girls who were just as quick to jump in bed with men as she was. After the umpteenth luxury product name-drop, I wanted to go to Debauve &amp; Gallais just so I could throw an expensive projectile at her head in a particularly poignant display of irony - also added hilarity, Madi speaks of Sulpice Debauve the way Trump spoke of Frederick Douglass, implying that he continues his great work to this day, lol.<br><br><br><br>The disappointing climax was the cherry on this disappointment sundae. I'm sorry that I was not more impressed with this book, because the premise really did sound interesting, but so many other authors have run with the "rich kids hiding a deadly secret" premise and done it one better, and honestly, I'd rather just watch <i>Hana Yori Dango</i>, because as far as I'm concerned, that story is the OG. Many thanks to Meggie for participating in this BR with me. You should check out <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2382784983" rel="nofollow noopener">her review</a>.<br><br><br><br>1 star</span>
  <a data-text-id="4361629076415964884" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1934202406" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1934202406" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6750905423272230950">I've just changed my review to 5 stars! Why you ask? Because my brain is still going on about this book. I am STILL thinking about it while reading another. Amo... honey child... you have once again created a winner!!<br/><br/>************************************************************<br/><br/>What was that???<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393309248ra/8692455.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>No seriously. What the heck did I just read???<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451745563ra/17597630.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Even though I thought I had a pretty good idea of what to expect, I now realize I didn't know shit!! I'm beyond mindblown. I'm mind-obliterated!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488860906ra/22161428.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>THE SILVER SWAN </span>
  <span id="freeText6750905423272230950" style="display:none">I've just changed my review to 5 stars! Why you ask? Because my brain is still going on about this book. I am STILL thinking about it while reading another. Amo... honey child... you have once again created a winner!!<br><br>************************************************************<br><br>What was that???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393309248ra/8692455.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No seriously. What the heck did I just read???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451745563ra/17597630.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though I thought I had a pretty good idea of what to expect, I now realize I didn't know shit!! I'm beyond mindblown. I'm mind-obliterated!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488860906ra/22161428.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>THE SILVER SWAN was a YA book that was absolutely <b>
  <u>NOT</u>
</b> for young adults. I don't care what the author said, I'm not allowing my children or any other teenage children I know read this. Nope. Not til they're older. Nosiree Bob. It was a story about 17 year olds who acted and behaved way beyond their years. I did some crazy shit when I was 17-18, but these kids took it to a whole other level of cray. Was it because of the money? The lifestyle? Their upbringing? Who the heck knows, but it made for a truly captivating read.<br><br>Madison and her father have relocated and once again she's the new girl at school. But her past has followed her all the way to The Hamptons. She luckily finds a fast friend in Tatum, but catches the eyes of The Elite Kings Club, a group of bad boys at the school, one of which is her new step-brother. The leader of the pack, Bishop, can't seem to leave her alone and she finds herself equally obsessed with him. And so the games begin.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488860906ra/22161429.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Madison was a little wannabe badass but I loved her snark and her attitude. However, she was a touch too naive when I consider how bright she seemed in many areas of her life. And she was gullible which made for some interesting times of me laughing at her (no, not with her) from the sidelines. It was Bishop who really kept me reading. He snagged me, hook, line and sinker. Despite his secrecy, his meanness, his crudeness and his utter disregard for anyone's feelings, I wanted more of him. Every time he did something to screw with Madison, I was busy trying (I'm still trying) to figure out his motives.<br><br>So here I am... at the end of this book... the story is unfinished... and I still have absolutely no clue what the heck was going on!! I still don't even know what this story was about. What I do know is that I <b>
  <u>WILL</u>
</b> be looking forward to the next book because I need answers!!<br><br><i>Release Date:</i> March 7, 2017<br><i>Genre:</i> Dark YA (not a romance) Romance<br><i>POV:</i> Heroine - 1st person<br><i>Steam:</i> 3.5 out of 5<br><i>Book Type:</i> Book One of The Elite Kings Club series<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487540050i/22024462.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2739870589" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4502619451096912147"><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=2vdqxj6' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551992408i/27169831._SX540_.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><b>THE SILVER SWAN:</b> Is the first full length New Adult novel in Amo Jones ‘Elite Kings Club’ series. <br/><br/>Newly arrival in town, its seventeen year old Madison (aka Madi) Montgomery’s first day at ‘Riverside Preparatory Academy. <i> “My dad moved us across state, because he found ‘the one.’ I’m beginning to think he can’t count. This would be his third ‘the one’ since my mum’s passing.” </i> It seems her past has followed her. Everyone’s heard the whispers, she’s the girl whose mum murdered her dad’s girlf</span>
  <span id="freeText4502619451096912147" style="display:none"><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2vdqxj6" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551992408i/27169831._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>THE SILVER SWAN:</b> Is the first full length New Adult novel in Amo Jones ‘Elite Kings Club’ series. <br><br>Newly arrival in town, its seventeen year old Madison (aka Madi) Montgomery’s first day at ‘Riverside Preparatory Academy. <i> “My dad moved us across state, because he found ‘the one.’ I’m beginning to think he can’t count. This would be his third ‘the one’ since my mum’s passing.” </i> It seems her past has followed her. Everyone’s heard the whispers, she’s the girl whose mum murdered her dad’s girlfriend before topping herself off. <br><br>So she’s beyond surprised when she’s befriended by a girl named Tatum, she also catches the eye of Bishop, the ring leader of the ‘Elite Kings Club.’ No one knows much really about the club only that apparently it has something to do with blood and their family linage. <i>“They’re like this undercover exclusive club. No one really knows what happens in this club, or who all the members really are, but it has to do with blood and your family lineage, apparently.”</i> <br><br>Tatum warns Madi to stay as far away from them as possible. You don’t mess with these guys. These guys are shrouded in darkness. You can feel it seeping out of their pores. They are dangerous. Never to be trusted. Never let your guard down around them. <br><br>So many questions<br>So many empty answers<br>So many promises<br>So many lies <br>They all started adding up!!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=k2xxcw" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551992408i/27169830.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>By a phone call she receives by her father, she learns that her fathers new bride’s son Nate will be moving into the manor, he attends the same school as Madi, it also seems like he’s part of the exclusive club. So for Madi to stay away from these boys was going to be near impossible. <br><br>The Silver Swan packed a lot of punch for the length, without me realising it I was hooked, as soon as I started this I couldn’t put it down, lately I’ve been binge reading highschool teen novels and this hit the right spot, without a second thought I purchased the next book.<br><br>Whilst reading this you could feel something lurking in the background awaiting the right moment to pounce, to take you unawares, the suspense, the cat and mouse games these A-wholes played just intrigued my interest even more. The angst levels spiked more each chapter. I wasn't sure where the author was going to lead me because answers were never given to us freely, like a puzzle we had to piece it together with the tidbits the author gave us.<br><br>Then BAM the last chapter was a whole plot twist.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2ir3yw5" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1515209538i/24840577.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2a0guva" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1515981059i/24879210._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br> <blockquote> <div>

Here's my rants:<br/><br/>Based on the blurb:<br/><br/><i>Madison Montgomery comes from money and power, but when someone close to her commits the ultimate crime, Madison must live with her tainted name for the rest of her life.</i> <b><-- Why is her name reminds me of Emma Ro</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3487848268221736448" style="display:none"><b>2* <i><u>unpopular and spoiler</u></i> STARS!</b><br><br>My first read from Amo Jones and I still didn't understand about it. I really need "high-level" imagination for this story. Absolutely speechless. I need to divided between reality and fantasy because it was confusing AF. Here's my rants:<br><br>Based on the blurb:<br><br><i>Madison Montgomery comes from money and power, but when someone close to her commits the ultimate crime, Madison must live with her tainted name for the rest of her life.</i> <b>&lt;-- Why is her name reminds me of Emma Roberts from AHS: Coven? Coincidental much. Pft. Her mother kill herself with Madison's gun. Apparently this family has hunting for a hobby.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489599041ra/22230900.gif" width="400" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>When she begins Riverside Preparatory Academy, the private school her father has swept her into in The Hamptons, she hopes for a fresh start.</i> &lt;-- <b>Everyone knows about the suicide. Then, Madison gain a new friend, Tatum who warn her about the ELITE KING'S CLUB. Madison also a self-proclaimed as a person who didn't like interact but the truth was far from it. *rolleyes*</b><br><br>*Until this point, it's really has similarity with Paper Princess. Out of nowhere girl, an elite fuckboi gang, and female sidekick. Except, Madison is super rich. Her father married for the third times and she has a step-brother, Nate whose also from the club.<br><br>Back to the blurb: <i>What she wasn't hoping for was the pack of bad boys who run the school; ten, to be exact. When Madison gains the attention of their leader, Bishop Vincent Hayes, a whole new world that she didn't think existed is exposed to her. A whole world that starts and ends with The Elite Kings Club and these boys, are about to flip her world upside down.</i> <b>&lt;-- It has Corrupt vibe. Also her step-brother, Nate is one of the club member. Apparently, the leader, Bishop owns the school.<br><br>Conclusion: </b><br>1. For "introvert" girl, Madison is super noisy. She has big mouth and a bit judgmental also slut shamming. There is a different between really a SLUT and sexually active. Bitch please... The first time she saw Bishop, she's instantly wet. All the guy from ELITE KING'S CLUB are flawless and perfect.<br><br>2. Out of nowehere, the ELITE KING'S CLUB started to bully Madison with riddles and non-sense. They're also harassed her many times. Terrorized her. Groped her and stuff. And then, call it as a game? Sick fuck. Eww... She also given pet name by them, Kitty. . .<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489600832ra/22231076.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>3. This Bishop guy is super creepy. He always stare at her (like Edward Cullen to Bella if you watch Twilight). He's grumpy, brooding and all the shit. Suddenly, he decided to 'play' with Madison. Bishop love to order her around and Madison like a puppy always follow him.<br><br>4. Madison spread her legs easily for Bishop. And after that, she became naive. She wants his attention but Bishop claimed to use her for sex. Err... You know the rest. FYI, it happened again. Multiple times in the future. I didn't feel their chemistry. AT ALL!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444338497ra/16485586.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>5. There are a lot of sex in this story (No orgy, thanks). Madison with this guy, Tatum with that guy, etc. What's disgust me about her, she tongue-kissed her step brother, Nate who fucked both her friends. Holy shite! Sorry, I'm not the type who hop around with other guys. Too slutty while she hope for Bishop will 'care' about her. Also Nate and Madison started to bitching with their non-sense feeling.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474572693ra/20618122.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Well, I don't know what's the ELITE KING'S CLUB purpose. Really. All they did until the end only for sex and bully-slash-almost rape. Some of them pointed out how rough the sex will be. With choking and bruising. Seriously... for a high school? <br><br>The plot has so many loose ends. Like I said, there is no purpose except they're just fooling around and scaring Madison. However, the ending is the one bothered me the most. Some kind of MAGICAL. I almost thought this is a paranormal/fantasy. The +1 star award is for me because I managed to finish it. Whew.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489600625ra/22231054.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1938053076" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1938053076" />
    <a title="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7530032-jessica-angie-jessica-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508375424p2/7530032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1938053076?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" href="/user/show/7530032-jessica-angie-jessica-s-dreamy-reads">Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1938053076" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2199355118963022195">This book was actually painful to try to get through. If I'm being completely honest, I wanted to DNF fairly early on but I didn't think I could write a fair review without finishing it so I forced myself to skim to the end. I know, I know... Its just a quirk of mine that doesn't allow me to quit. <br/><br/>I'm not even going to get into the plot because I just found it all too over the top ridiculous. There were elements in this book that reminded me of a few other books I've read before whether intentio</span>
  <span id="freeText2199355118963022195" style="display:none">This book was actually painful to try to get through. If I'm being completely honest, I wanted to DNF fairly early on but I didn't think I could write a fair review without finishing it so I forced myself to skim to the end. I know, I know... Its just a quirk of mine that doesn't allow me to quit. <br /><br />I'm not even going to get into the plot because I just found it all too over the top ridiculous. There were elements in this book that reminded me of a few other books I've read before whether intentional or not and, frankly, if you're going to jump on a bandwagon, you really need to SELL IT. I was not sold. I was so far from sold. <br /><br />I couldn't connect with any of these characters (And there's a million or so to choose from.) The writing felt amateur and the dialogue was so unnatural and redundant. This book could have used some serious editing, but even with that, the execution of this story was just... lacking. I'm not sure if this is this author's debut or not, maybe they just haven't quite found their stride, but the writing was not polished, the style was just all over the place.<br /><br />I'm a reader that needs believability, even in my fiction, and there was nothing natural or believable about any of the interactions these characters had with each other. I can bite the bullet and take a book for what it is when it starts to head into crazytown, but an author needs to sell it. Pull me in somehow, connect me with a character, intrigue me with some element of the plot. There was just nothing here. There's no character development, no depth. There's just a lot of ridiculous arguments between even more ridiculous characters, a lot of throwing everything against the wall to see what would stick, a lot of unnecessary details and an exorbitant number of side characters that served no real purpose other than to maybe distract the reader from the fact that there's nothing compelling about this book. I was over it before of even began.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2199355118963022195" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1833493554" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1833493554" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1833493554?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sabrina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sabrina" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina">Sabrina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=lose-the-panties-hot">lose-the-panties-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=college-new-adult-romance">college-new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=hanging-from-a-cliffy">hanging-from-a-cliffy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=arc-edelweiss-netgalley">arc-edelweiss-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=give-it-to-me-dark-and-twisted">give-it-to-me-dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1833493554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17397161405425461"><b>NOW LIVE!</b><br/><a href='http://amzn.to/2mC8zo7' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kindle</a>*<a href='http://amzn.to/2nb5pUL' rel='nofollow noopener'>Paperback</a><br/><br/>This review has me pulling my hair out because I have so much I <u>want</u> to say but so much that I <u>can't</u> say without ruining this story. I loved this book so hard and I easily became very invested in these characters. I don't think my heart stopped pounding once while I was reading it because everything just got so insane. I don't think I can even begin to describe the types of fucked up this book was because there's just too much I would need to explain. Not that I actually</span>
  <span id="freeText17397161405425461" style="display:none"><b>NOW LIVE!</b><br><a href="http://amzn.to/2mC8zo7" rel="nofollow noopener">Kindle</a>*<a href="http://amzn.to/2nb5pUL" rel="nofollow noopener">Paperback</a><br><br>This review has me pulling my hair out because I have so much I <u>want</u> to say but so much that I <u>can't</u> say without ruining this story. I loved this book so hard and I easily became very invested in these characters. I don't think my heart stopped pounding once while I was reading it because everything just got so insane. I don't think I can even begin to describe the types of fucked up this book was because there's just too much I would need to explain. Not that I actually know anything since I'm still left with so many questions that have me ready to stalk the hell out of Amo Jones and beg her to tell me what's going to happen in the next book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488756414ra/22151098.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You know that feeling when you're watching a horror movie and you just know that something is about to jump out and make your heart stop for a second? That's the feeling of anticipation I had the whole entire time while reading this. From the very beginning we're taken on this journey of craziness and the crazy-train never stops after that. You'll be questioning everything that happens and you'll be suspicious of ever single person that is introduced. It's brilliant! <br><br>I honestly didn't know what was going to happen in this story, and that isn't something that happens a lot. Be prepared for everything is the only advice i can give you for going into this one. I can't recommend this book fast enough and I hope a lot of people will pick it up and give it a try. <br><blockquote>
  <pre><u>The Silver Swan Playlist:</u><br>Until the Levee - Joy Williams<br>Marked For Death - Emma Ruth Rundle <br>Go - Shana Falana<br>No light, no light - Florence + The Machine <br>Raise Hell - Dorothy <br>Amelia - Skott <br>It Will Come Back - Hozier</pre>
</blockquote><br><i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_1938449856" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1938449856" />
    <a title="Rook" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/65836866-rook"><img alt="Rook" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1938449856?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rook" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rook" href="/user/show/65836866-rook">Rook</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1938449856" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14032276842785664318">a crapload of these 5 star reviews are from people who bandwagon this author.<br/><br/>The cover is absolutely gorgeous. and that's basically the only good thing about this book.<br/><br/>It needs an editor. Badly. And there's a mid section that has formatting issues. This book was brought to my attention when this author "attacked" a blogger and made a huge spectacle when her book was compared to similar books. Her immature friends hopped on board and dared anyone to hate this book. to read it and then make compar</span>
  <span id="freeText14032276842785664318" style="display:none">a crapload of these 5 star reviews are from people who bandwagon this author.<br /><br />The cover is absolutely gorgeous. and that's basically the only good thing about this book.<br /><br />It needs an editor. Badly. And there's a mid section that has formatting issues. This book was brought to my attention when this author "attacked" a blogger and made a huge spectacle when her book was compared to similar books. Her immature friends hopped on board and dared anyone to hate this book. to read it and then make comparisons. <br /><br />So, I did.<br /><br />Completely unimpressed. Here's why. (There aren't any spoilers in this review.)<br /><br />1. The writing was very amateur and for her to be a seasoned author, I didn't get it.<br /><br />2. Madi was a TSTL heroine. She was turned on by almost every boy she came in contact with. Her way of thinking made me want to choke slam her into a wall.<br /><br />3. Cliche rich bad boys? Check.<br /><br />4. Uneccessary side characters? Yup.<br /><br />5. Unrealistic events that made things convenient? Yup.<br /><br />This book was not twisted or dark. I'm lmao at those statements. It's of Self entitled rich assholes who mess with another rich assholes who has zero brain cells and acts like a hoochie. How can something be twisted and mind game ish if the entire book was just them screwing with her. No shit you shouldn't trust them. stupid girl. and fyi. I was a teen not that long ago. We don't act like this. <br /><br />The whole 'Silver Sean's thing was weiiird. like didn't fit with this story at all. There is so much going on. The plot was all over the place. irritating.<br /><br />Now....this author CLEARLY took the story line of Corrupted, paper princess, ( awesome books btw.) and worked it how she wanted. Shall we compare?<br /><br />1. The group of boys in masks.-corrupted<br />2. The group of boys torturing our poor Mary sue.-all of them<br />3.Rich little assholes that revolve around a H.S setting-all of them.<br />4. MONTGOMERY- the last name of rich kids in Paper Princess<br />5.Naming every single song-corrupted<br />6.Missing a mother-paper princess<br />7.Heroine and another man-corrupted<br />8.the step brother thing-papaer princess<br />9.New girl at school-paper princess<br />10.Mean girl who used to like the male lead/does-paper princess<br />11.Ends with girl running away because she's been hurt-paper princess<br />12.Girl is supposed to be tough and kickass-Paper princess.<br /><br />I could go on and on and on. Did she just take paper princess and add in a small bit of Corrupted? This was some of the most unoriginal shit I've ever seen. And she didn't execute it well. At all! And her next book the last name is ROYAL. I'm lol. I've read another a her books after this and was as equally unimpressed. She does not write 'Dark' books. <br /><br />I am not a blogger or associated with one. I bought this book from Amazon.</span>

  <span id="freeText5046084685558507494" style="display:none"><b>REVIEW EDITED 02.04.2017</b><br>Lol, after a lot of thought - okay, I won't lie; after a lot of sleep, I finally decided to go back and change the rating/stars from three stars to two. This is because I got through the book, and even though it did have potential, it still wasn't the best read out there. And I really had a problem with the lack of depth in the story/writing...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>This book had so much potential</b>. I liked the concept of the series, the <b>Elite Kings Club</b> and <b>The Silver Swan</b>, so it's obvious I had no problem with the story. I did, however, had a bit of a problem with the writing. I didn't feel the connection between the characters, I didn't feel <b>Madison Maree Montgomery</b>'s friendship with <b>Tillie</b> and <b> Tatum</b>. I didn't feel her brother love for <b>Nate</b> and I still cannot get over how easily she forgives and trust them. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But you will be dead by the time this is done. The timer starts now. The games have just begun.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Nor did I understand how she could trust <b>Bishop Vincent Hayes</b>. Sure, Bishop was <b>hot as hell</b>, and definitely <b>knows his way around</b> in bed, but he did nothing to gain Madi's trust. <b>Overall</b>, this book was some serious potential and <b>the sex scenes were hot</b>. Other than that, it was rather <i>meh</i>. Oh and the book reminded me a lot of <b>Fallen Crest High</b> series by <b>Tijan</b>, just that F.C.H was better. Way better. Also, this book was very predictable.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“To stories that fuck you so good you’ll need a cigarette. This is one of those stories.”</i>
  </b>

I began questioning my <b>morals</b> and the kind of <b>debauchery</b> I like reading about. There's sexual situations, obscene language, shaming, violence/murder, and sexual harassme</span>
  <span id="freeText201596518969459102" style="display:none">Oh, what the heck.. 5 stars!<br><br>Here is my <b>official warning</b> before anyone begins this series because I don't want anyone being misled. <b>THIS IS NOT YA.</b> I need to make that very, very clear. <b>THIS IS DARK AND VERY SERIOUSLY MESSED UP.</b> This story is <b>twisted</b> and NOT for those who are uncomfortable with their <b>hard limits</b> being challenged. I began questioning my <b>morals</b> and the kind of <b>debauchery</b> I like reading about. There's sexual situations, obscene language, shaming, violence/murder, and sexual harassment. There are secrets, lies, jealously, and deceit -- and situations that spoke to my own feelings of uncertainty, fear, guilt, and shame.<br><br>What the......<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1558040879ra/27524992.gif" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's insane. It's dark. It's hot. My emotions became conflicted. I couldn't stop reading. I couldn't look away. The plot was sooo goood -- fast-paced, fascinating, and wicked. The writing and execution is far from perfect but this is one of those times when I'm letting it slide. It kept me in <b>constant suspense</b>. It gave me a freaking thrill. What is wrong with me??? I don't know how to clearly explain the fuckery that occurred!! I JUST DON'T EVEN KNOW. <b>I felt disturbed and thrilled all within the same sentence.</b> Dear God, I'm going to hell. I need a soul cleanse. I also want to make it clear that I, in no way, condone the behaviors and actions of these characters.<br><br><b>So what is this book about? (no spoilers)</b><br><br>The Silver Swan is book 1 in the series, Elite Kings Club.<br><b>
  <blockquote>“Hello, Madison. You may not know us, but we know you. We want to play a game. Here’s what happens if you lose….”</blockquote>
</b><br>Madison comes from money and power, but when someone close to her commits the ultimate crime, Madison must live with her tainted name for the rest of her life. When she begins Riverside Preparatory Academy, the private school her father has swept her into in The Hamptons, she hopes for a fresh start. What she wasn't hoping for was the pack of bad boys who run the school; ten, to be exact. When Madison gains the attention of their leader, Bishop Vincent Hayes, a whole new world that she didn't think existed is exposed to her. A whole world that starts and ends with The Elite Kings Club and these boys, are about to flip her world upside down. Secrets are overflowing and family lies are about to be exposed.<br><br>Madison quickly finds herself in a downward spiral into sex and drugs -- secrets and jealously.<br><b>
  <blockquote>A side of me, a side I haven’t ever opened before, wants to fuck the soul out of him.</blockquote>
</b><br>I related to Madison, which is why I connected to the story being told. In high school, I found myself falling into a similar deep, dark lifestyle that I am surprised I survived. I didn't care about what I did, where I went, or who I was with. I was screaming for any kind of affection and attention, and so I gave freely to anyone who met those needs. I, like Madison, often questioned what the hell I was doing WHILE in the moment.... knowing it was wrong. I felt in control but often not at the same time. I didn't know how to get myself out of the hole I was digging. I understood Madison's fear and helplessness as she tried to gain control any way she could.<br><br>Let's talk about the Kings for a moment. They make up the Elite Kings Club, an undercover exclusive club that has to do with blood and lineage. They are intense, sinister, edgy, cold, callous, and frightening-- but they have an alluring quality to them. They get their hands dirty.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1560012723ra/27638623.gif" width="325" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They are untamed and spoiled and playing a part which they DO NOT want to be playing, all because they were raised into it by tradition, money, and greed. These boys are wicked players and absolutely, fucking insane.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449848669ra/17347889.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>His fingers dig into my hip bones as he runs his hand down from the back of my neck. “Fuck, you’ve got a sexy fucking spine.”<br><br>“I wonder,” he whispers, pressing one finger inside of me before his mouth comes to my pussy from behind. “What it would be like to take it apart.”</blockquote>
</b><br>Like... WHAT THE HECK. What the actual fuck??? This is just a taste of what is to be expected from these characters.<br><br>Things take a sinister turn near the end. Beware of the unapologetic cliffhanger as well. It's been a few days since I finished book one and I cannot stop thinking about the characters. They've already invaded a dream and my favorite song at the moment has somehow become this books anthem.</span>
  <a data-text-id="201596518969459102" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4384424009737757439">You know one of those books everyone loves (five stars and rave reviews) and you find yourself within the few people who seem to hate it?? this is one of those books. I was so looking forward to reading this book because Corrupt, Royals and the Fallen Crest Series are books that i loved and there are similarities with this book (from the blurb) but alas, that's where the similarities end. Here goes<br/>1. All the characters in this book are immature. <br/>2. I couldn't connect with any of the characters. </span>
  <span id="freeText4384424009737757439" style="display:none">You know one of those books everyone loves (five stars and rave reviews) and you find yourself within the few people who seem to hate it?? this is one of those books. I was so looking forward to reading this book because Corrupt, Royals and the Fallen Crest Series are books that i loved and there are similarities with this book (from the blurb) but alas, that's where the similarities end. Here goes<br />1. All the characters in this book are immature. <br />2. I couldn't connect with any of the characters. <br />3. h practically gets it on with all the boys and gets turned on with each one. Um. I don't know if it's the unrealistic expectation that other romance novels have set for me but the h isn't supposed to feel hot and bothered if anyone but the H kisses her. Oh well. <br />4. I was soo confused in some instances that i had to flip back to make sure I didn't miss a page. <br />5. I FEEL LET DOWN BECAUSE I WAS LOOKING FORWARD TO READING THIS BOOK! <br />6. The blurb promised "dark" but this ain't even close to dark. You want dark, read Celia Aaron's Acquisition Series (you're welcome)<br />7. I AM SAD BY HOW LET DOWN I FEEL BY THIS BOOK. YOU CANNOT UNDERSTAND. <br />8. I wanted it to be the love child of Corrupt and Fallen Crest. <br />9. I FEEL HEARTBROKEN but I'll get the second book of the series to see how it progresses. Thats how much i want to love this series. I just hope the writer gets a good editor and beta reader(s) Thanks and God bless. <br />Oooh i just remembered one of the things that irked me, the writer gives us the artist name and song of every song that Madi hears. What happened to having a list of playlist at the beginning or end of the book?? And I don't think i would have minded if it was done maybe twice or three times, but nope it goes on and on and on. Sigh. </span>

<div id="review_1935818777" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1935818777" />
    <a title="Raven_Blake (dreamy addictions)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6187625-raven-blake-dreamy-addictions"><img alt="Raven_Blake (dreamy addictions)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1335409224p2/6187625.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1935818777?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Raven_Blake (dreamy addictions)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Raven_Blake (dreamy addictions)" href="/user/show/6187625-raven-blake-dreamy-addictions">Raven_Blake (dreamy addictions)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6187625-raven-blake-dreamy-addictions?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6187625-raven-blake-dreamy-addictions?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6187625-raven-blake-dreamy-addictions?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6187625-raven-blake-dreamy-addictions?shelf=na-contemporary">na-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1935818777" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12944889206393493430">Same Review Also Posted In MY Blog:<a href='https://dreamyaddictions.wordpress.com/2017/03/24/the-silver-swan-the-elite-kings-club-1-by-amo-jones-review/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dreamy Addictions</a><br/><br/><i>
  <b>Riddle me this...<br/>“I am neither dead, nor alive, and I’m not something little Madison can hide.<br/>But you will be dead, by the time this is done...<br/>the timer starts now, and the games have just begun…”</b>
</i><br/><br/><b>WHAT DA F*CK DID I JUST READ?</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410050144ra/11056916.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“Hello, Madison. You may not know us, but we know you. We want to play a game. Here`s what happens if you lose…”</b>
</i><br/><br/>I can’t describe how much fucked up this book is and all the characters are totally insane. I was very</span>
  <span id="freeText12944889206393493430" style="display:none">Same Review Also Posted In MY Blog:<a href="https://dreamyaddictions.wordpress.com/2017/03/24/the-silver-swan-the-elite-kings-club-1-by-amo-jones-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">Dreamy Addictions</a><br><br><i>
  <b>Riddle me this...<br>“I am neither dead, nor alive, and I’m not something little Madison can hide.<br>But you will be dead, by the time this is done...<br>the timer starts now, and the games have just begun…”</b>
</i><br><br><b>WHAT DA F*CK DID I JUST READ?</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410050144ra/11056916.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“Hello, Madison. You may not know us, but we know you. We want to play a game. Here`s what happens if you lose…”</b>
</i><br><br>I can’t describe how much fucked up this book is and all the characters are totally insane. I was very intrigued when I read the synopsis of this book and the author’s warning note has done nothing but pique my interest. I also loved the beautiful cover of this book. This book totally blew my fucking mind with all its mind fuckery. I honestly didn’t liked any of the characters in this book because every one is pretty much screwed up in their own way but it really didn’t hindered my enjoyablity. Though this book was set around high school students it’s definitely not for young adults. This is my first book from Amo Jones so I really don’t know what to expect from her but I knew this is going to be another dark and twisted story. After finishing this book, all I can say that it is not too dark as expected but definitely a twisted and thrilling tale. I think this book is not for everyone because you’re either going to hate it, love it or maybe get repulsed by it.<br><br><i>
  <b>“This is all a game, kitty. Bishop, me, the Kings – it’s a game, but it’s a death match.”</b>
</i><br><br>The story follows Madison Montgomery whose mother killed herself with Madison’s gun after killing the woman her father was having an affair with. When Madison’s father remarries, she moves to a new city and attends a private school named Riverside Preparatory school. Madison wants to start a new life at the new school but it seems her past makes it pretty much impossible for that to happen. At the first day of her school, she gets the attention of the bad boys of the school who owns the school and they’re also rumored to be members of a super secret club called “The Elite Kings Club”. She gets intrigued by everyone in the club especially Bishop, the leader of the group who can’t stop taking his cold eyes away from her. Her new friend Tatum warns her to stay away from the boys but she doesn’t know she’s pretty too late for that because they already had their eyes on her. Madison knew these guys are trouble and when she enters their world they turn her life pretty much upside down. It seems everyone keeping secrets from her that might be something to do with her. When all the lies and family secrets are finally exposed can Madison be the same again? Can she handle the truth?<br><br><i>
  <b>“The students of Riverside Prep are just pawns in their sick and twisted games. They own this school, Madison.”</b>
</i><br><br>All the characters in this book are flawed and honestly, I didn’t liked any of them but I did enjoyed reading about them. Madison is a fiesty, stubborn and sassy character who don’t give a shit about what everyone thinks. She might be not my favorite female protagonist but it doesn’t mean I hate her either. Maybe I would’ve liked her more if she didn’t acted like a slutty character sometimes. The step sibling relationship between Nate and Madison seemed pretty disturbing to me because he calls her sister but he doesn’t mind ogling her body and making out with her*gag*. All the guys in this book are fucking A-holes. Bishop is totally alpha male, arrogant and dark. He always has a hard edged personality and has some sort of obsession with Maddy. The hate to lust or hate to love relationship between Maddy and Bishop is quite explosive and their hot chemistry is definitely off the charts. As for the secondary characters, we have Nate,Tatum, Tillie, Brantley, Carter, Abel, Hunter, Chase, Eli and Cash. Nate is Madison’s new step brother and also a total manwhore who loves to tease Maddy. Brantely is pretty hateful guy who has a mean and rude personality. I thought Carter is a good guy but he turns out to be another arrogant asshole. Tatum and Tillie are Madison’s new friends and I really enjoyed the friendship between these three.<br><br> <i>
  <b>“They are not the boys I suspected they were. They`re the kind of monsters you warn people about. Not naïve children, but adults. The kind who lie, cheat, manipulate, seduce, and kill, just to get what they want. They`re the kind you run from.”</b>
</i><br><br><br>The plot is thrilling, suspenseful, mysterious and engaging. Though the plot felt quite unrealistic, the story captivated me from the start. The pacing was perfect with no dull moments. As the mystery slowly unveils with each chapter, It was easy to predict how it’s going to end and the second half has literally kept me on the edge of my seat until the end. Seriously, this book was hard to put down even for a sec and I just finished it in one sitting. I liked the writing style of this book. It’s too bad that this book was told in Madison’s POV because I really wanted to know what’s going on in Bishop’s mind. Nevertheless, it made me even more excited to know the truth. This book actually reminded me of Paper princess but this one is far more twisted than that.<br><br><i>
  <b>“In this world, secrets are weapons, kitty. It’s what stands between us and six feet underground.”</b>
</i><br><br>Overall, I loved it! It was a thrilling read filled with suspense, mystery, hot steamy romance and drama. I already knew this was going to end with a shocking cliffhanger and now I’m dying to know what’s gonna happen next.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12944889206393493430" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="KELLY (THE QUEEN OF RAMBLING)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KELLY (THE QUEEN OF RAMBLING)" href="/user/show/65714349-kelly-the-queen-of-rambling">KELLY (THE QUEEN OF RAMBLING)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1934890763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9557215432371473394">I'm only just setting up my goodreads account today as I use Booklikes I am in the process of transferring my reviews over today. But I pinched my darling husbands credit card and went and purchased this as soon as I saw it go live.<br/><br/>I'm not affiliated with a blog or have any connection with this author in any way, but I've seen alot of stigma connected to this book and had to check it out for myself, some good, some not so good. <br/><br/>There were a few flags popping up whilst I was reading this, first i</span>
  <span id="freeText9557215432371473394" style="display:none">I'm only just setting up my goodreads account today as I use Booklikes I am in the process of transferring my reviews over today. But I pinched my darling husbands credit card and went and purchased this as soon as I saw it go live.<br /><br />I'm not affiliated with a blog or have any connection with this author in any way, but I've seen alot of stigma connected to this book and had to check it out for myself, some good, some not so good. <br /><br />There were a few flags popping up whilst I was reading this, first it states it is YA I wouldn't recommend this to a young adult as it does go dark and twisted, amongst other things. I am glad I took the plunge to read this after my young niece asked if she could read this, the answer to that is a big fat flabby NO!! <br /><br />I've not read anything by this author before so I can't compare her previous works to what is in front of me, and what is in front of me is poor penmanship, the storyline is missing a lot of key elements to allow it to flow freely as say a seasoned author, her use of words though she tries to throw in some clever big words they don't match with her characters mindset or age category she has placed them in, so I found the connection there lacking. If she had an experienced beta reader under her belt and put this through an editor before hitting publish this book would be soaring. Take out over the top promiscuous sexual scenes too and it would be more YA as it is it's coming under the contemporary romance radar. <br />. <br />It is also borderline similar to two other books I have read (The Royals and Corrupt) but she has switched it up a notch that not many will notice unless you've read those books.<br /><br />I think being completely honest the only good thing this book has going for it is the cover.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('iaUlR/+G/YBFUiLTHp9XwsYDtJMGwsvspkFSSutl8f2k97K3lDSF1vlQo4mzDT0/5d1rQAaBhl/qOp2PsR0KcA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Sz0BnEjDdv+C1Z4F0BK98/D0vgMSs30i3aVC9dIpfOVmb5ZsI3EOqT7XH199gNcO0yph0BLwMJGR3o0wiFGHaA==')})
  }

This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
